 wo bhi 40-42 degree kii garmi main

 > anuchhed 35A se jammu kashmir ko ye adhikaar mila he ki wo kise apana sthai nivasee maane or kise nahin
 > The Government of Jammu and Kashmir considers those who settled in Kashmir before 14 May 1954
 > aise sthai nivaasiyon ko jameen kharidne, rojgaar paane or sarkari yojanaon main vishesh adhikaar mili hai
 > a resident of another state of the country cannot settle in Jammu and Kashmir as a permanent resident
 > duusare rajyon ke nivasee naa kashmir main jameen kharid sakate hai, naa rajya sarkaar unhen naukari de sakati he
 > If a woman from Jammu and Kashmir marries a person from another state in India, her rights are taken away
 > umr abdulla kii shaadi bhi rajya se baahar kii mahila se hui he, lekin unke bacchon ko rajya ke saare adhikaar hasil hai
 Omar Abdullah's sister Sara Abdullah is denied property rights after marrying a person from outside the state
 samvidhan ke anuchhed 370 ke tahat hi joda gaya tha anuchhed 35e> anuchhed 370 kii vajah se jammu kashmir ke nagarikon ke paas dohari naagarikta he
 > Due to Article 370, there is a separate flag and separate constitution in Jammu and Kashmir
 > isaki vajah se kashmir main vidhansabha kaa kaarykaal 6 saal kaa hota he, jabaki anya rajyon main 5 saal kaa hota he
 > Due to this, the Indian Parliament has very limited powers to make laws regarding Jammu and Kashmir
 > sansad main paas kanoon jammu kashmir main lagu nahin hote jaise naa shiksha kaa adhikaar, naa soochna kaa adhikaar
 > Neither reservation is available, nor does the law of minimum wage apply
 kya he iskaa kanoonee pahalu?> 2014 main ve da citigens naam ke ek NGO ne supreme court main arji lagaai thi
 > The petition challenged the validity of Article 35A and Article 370 of the Constitution
 > ye daleel di gai ki samvidhan banaate vakt kashmir ke aise vishesh darje kii koi baat nahin kahi gai thi
 > Even four members of the Constituent Assembly who drafted the Constitution were from Kashmir itself
 > anuchhed 370 tempreri praavdhaan tha, jo us vakt halaat saamaanya or loktantr majboot karne ke liye laayaa gaya tha
 > The framers of the Constitution did not think that provisions like 35A would be added in the name of Article 370
 > anuchhed 35 e us bhaavana par chot karata he jo ek bharat ke taur par puure desh ko jodta he
 > Lack of rights of citizens of other states in Jammu and Kashmir is against the basic rights of the Constitution
 kya he anuchhed 35 e kaa itihaas?> anuchhed 35A ko raashtrapati ke ek aadesh se samvidhan main saal 1954 main joda gaya tha
 > This order was issued on the advice of the then Prime Minister Jawaharlal Nehru's cabinet
 > isse do saal pehle 1952 main nehru or shaikh abdulla kaa dilli samjhauta hua tha
 > Under which Indian citizenship was enforced in the subjects of the state of Jammu and Kashmir
 > lekin anuchhed 35 e ko khaas taur par kashmir ke special states ko dikhaane ke liye laayaa gaya

 kyonki is par sansad main koi charchaa or bahes nahin hui

 khaane-pine kaa routine time par bana rahe iske liye jaruri he ki grosri shopping time par kii jaae
 Now when grocery shopping is important, it is necessary to know those things too, with the help of which you can make better shopping in less money and less time
 jaanate hai behatar grosri shopping ke ye jaruri 10 tips1) plan banaaenapako sunne main bhale hi yah ajeeb lage shopping par jate samay yah kabhi dyside na karen ki aapako kya-kya khareednaa he
 It is better to update the items in a list whenever you remember
 2) shopping list hameshaa apane saath le jaenksar dukaan par pahunch kar hamen pataa chalata he ki ham list ghar par hi bhul aaen he isiilie shoppig par jane se pehle hameshaa yaad se list saath rakh len
 This list becomes even more important when you have a limited time and at the same time you have to update all the things for the house
 3) saamaan kaa dukaanon ke mutabik group banaaenhameshaa saamaan ko ek group main baant len isse aapako pataa rahegaa ki kis dukaan main jaakar kya lenaa or aapako kul kitni alag-alag dukaanon par jane kii jarurat he
 You can save time with this better planning
 4) list se bhataken nahinaapane list kisi khaas vajah se banaai he isliye jaruri he ki aap us par tike rahen
 If you are honest about your list, then you will avoid the expense of waste
 5) thok main sirf jarurat kaa saamaan hiaksar ham ophers, chhot jaise lubhaavne prastaav kii vajah se kisi cheez ko zyada quantity main kharid lete hai
 You should always take care of variety so that you will not boil quickly and the bulk of goods will not be wasted
 6) ek hafte kii kharidari kaa menu banaaenrozaanaa kuch na kuch kharidne ke liye dukaan par jane se behatar he ki aap hafte bhar ke saamaan kii list ek saath bana len or usee ke mutabik saamaan khariden
 Also, decide the next shopping date
 isse ghar par achaanak saamaan khatm hone kii sthiti kaa saamana aapako nahin karnaa padegaa
 7) Do not shop at peak hours, always go shopping at a time when the crowd is less and the line for payment is small
 saath hi aapke paas bhi fursat ho
 We should try not to go shopping in the evening, night and Sunday afternoon
 is samay zyaadaatar log kharidari ke liye ikattha hote hai or samay kaa abhaav hone par aksar kuch na kuch lenaa chhot jaataa he
 8) Check expiry date Whenever you are buying a product, check the expiry date
 is baat ko bhi check karen ki packing main koi kharabi na ho
 Many times some items that are sold at a discount or low rate may be close to their expiry date or there may be a defect in their packing
 iskaa sidhaa-sa matlab yah he ki us cheez kii quality ke saath samjhauta kiya gaya he
 9) Go shopping with a friend, as far as possible, go shopping with a friend or neighbor who is health conscious and believes in healthy food
 shopping ke dauraan junk food ke opshan aasaani se aapako lalachaa dete hai
 Especially when there are offers like 'buy one get one free' with junk food
 aise samay main ye frends hi aapako aisi kharidari karne se rokte hai
 10) Understand the labels: Many products are packaged with words like Low Fat
 adhiktar inako dhang se samaj nahin pate hai
 Most low-fat foods have a high amount of sugar or salt added to taste
 khaane kaa saamaan kharidte samay usame maujuud calories ke lienutrishnal labals jarur padhein
 If something is low calorie, it does not mean that it is healthy too
 aapako calories vailu ke liye nahin, balki quality vailu ke liye khaanaa chahie

 ' saal 2017 main bitakwine chaaya rahaa
 The price of bitcoin rose a lot and at one time it reached 13 lakh rupees, so that from investors to economists could not live without being affected by it
 haalanki, iske baad isaki keemat ghatakar kareeb aadhi ho chuki he
 But while Bitcoin is being considered as a bad name, its basic technology 'blockchain' is being considered revolutionary for the future economy
 blockchen kii lokapriyata pichley saal hi badhani shuru ho gai he, lekin aisa mana ja rahaa he ki yah banking se lekar, aadhaar or chunaav pranali tak bhavishya ke bharat main krantikari badlaav laa sakati he
 What is blockchainblockchains are actually decentralized digital ledgers that form the basis of all types of crypto currencies
 digital soochnaaon ko copy nahin balki vitarit karne kii suvidha se blockchen technology ne nae tarah ke internet kaa aadhaar taiyaar kiya he
 Although it was invented for digital currency bitcoin, but now it has started focusing on other types of usage
 distributed public lager ke rup main kaary karte hue blockchen lenden kaa ek vikendrit or paardarshee tarika uplabdh karata he or isamen suraksha kaa str bhi kaaphi ooncha hota he
 Experts say that it is not just digital currency but it is much further than that
 yah internet se paraspar judi duniya main or vistaar kar saktaa he
 What are the advantages? The advantage of pairing of internet and blockchain will be that it will reduce the risk of hacking of data, because it will be able to store data through a chain of millions of computers
 blockchen kii ek pramukh visheshta yah hoti he ki yah vikendrit prakruti kaa hota he
 Unlike the technology currently used to keep records in banks, healthcare, government agencies, no intermediary is required to change the ledgers in the blockchain
 kisi blockchen main har yujar apane personal block kaa castodian hota he or jab bhi kisi block main badlaav kiya jaataa he to lager main apane aap badlaav ho jaataa he
 But if any other fake person wants to change it and the information entered by him about a block does not match, then the laser will not update
 is vajah se yah technology kaaphi surakshit he
 The blockchain is still in its early stages, but efforts to mainstream it have begun
 krypto karencys ke alaava kai tarah ke udyogon main blockchen technology ke istemaal kaa pareekshan shuru ho gaya he
 The banking sector is at the forefront
 jaalsaji se bachane or apane kaarobaar main behatari ke liye agle varshon main zyada se zyada bank blockchen kaa istemaal karenge
 Many banks abroad are testing blockchain-based cryptocurrency for money transfer
 america ke mani transfar diggaj manigram ne is bare main ripal se samjhauta kiya he
 It is believed that technology like blockchain based Ripple will reduce the time of cross border money transfer to just 2 to 3 seconds
 laagat or samay bachaane ke liye banking ke alaava duusare kai sector bhi blockchen technology kaa pareekshan shuru kar chuke hai
 What will change in India Blockchain technology can affect many things in our daily lives due to its decentralized nature
 yah technology kaaphi tej, surakshit or kifayati he
 Therefore in digitization it can prove to be quite suitable for government departments in countries like India
 aadhaar jaisi digital aadhaarit suvidhaon main blockchen technology kaaphi madadgaar ho sakati he
 There has been a lot of hue and cry about data leaks in Aadhaar, but the use of blockchain can solve this problem

 With the use of this technology, there will be no forgery in the case of voters

 pradhanmantri manmohan singh 26-27 march ko yojit parmaanu suraksha shikhar sammelan main hissaa lene ke liye shanivaar ko yahaan pahunch gaye
 He will be on an official visit to South Korea on 24-25 before the summit
 manmohan singh, duniya ke 57 netaaon ke saath parmaanu shikhar sammelan main hissaa lenge
 US President Barack Obama is also joining it
 duniya ke netaa parmaanu aatankwaad se paidaa ho rahe vaishvik khatre or samvedansheel parmaanu samagriyon va praudyogiki tak aatankwaadiyon ko pahunchane se rokane ke liye jaruri upayon par is sammelan main charchaa karenge
 In his statement in New Delhi on Friday before departure, Manmohan Singh called for maintaining high-level nuclear security to maintain public support in earning the benefits of nuclear power
 unhone kaha, "bharat apane urja sroton main vividhta laane va urja suraksha badhaane ke liye apane parmaanu bijli kaarykram kaa vistaar kar rahaa he

 " Singh said that the need for nuclear security has become relatively more important after the Fukushima tragedy in Japan last year

 Singh said, "I will tell you about my high priority related to nuclear security and nuclear non-proliferation there and my impeccable record in this regard
 main duniya ko parmaanu hathiyaaron se mukt banane ke prati bharat ke satat samarthan ko bhi rekhaankit karuunga
 "he said that during this time there will be an opportunity to meet many leaders from other countries who have reached the summit
 tippaniyan Singh said he is also looking forward to his bilateral meeting with South Korean President Lee Myung-bak

 Manmohan Singh will participate in the Nuclear Summit along with 57 world leaders
 isamen america raashtrapati baraak obama bhi shaamil ho rahe hai
 The world leaders will discuss the global threat posed by nuclear terrorism and the measures needed to prevent terrorists from accessing sensitive nuclear materials and technology
 prasthaan se pehle nai dilli main shuukravaar ko apane bayaan main manmohan singh ne parmaanu urja ke laabh arjeet karne main janata kaa samarthan banaae rakhane ke liye ucchstareey parmaanu suraksha banaae rakhane kaa aahvaan kiya tha
 He said, "india is expanding its nuclear power program to diversify its energy sources and increase energy security
" parmaanu urja ke phaaydon ke prati janata kaa samarthan hasil karne ke liye hamen unhen adhiktam parmaanu suraksha dene ke prati aashwast karnaa hoga
 " singh ne kaha tha ki pichley varsh japan main phukushima traasadee ke baad parmaanu suraksha kii aavashyaktaa apekshaakrit adhik mahatvapurn ho gai he
 He said that India has submitted a national report to strengthen the global nuclear security framework and it will be shared during the summit
 singh ne kaha, "main vahaan parmaanu suraksha va parmaanu aprasar se judi apni ucch praathamikta va is sambandh main apane bedaag record ke sambandh main bataaungaa
 i will also underline India's continued support for making the world free of nuclear weapons
 " unhone kaha ki is dauraan shikhar sammelan main pahunchane vaale anya deshon ke kai netaaon se bhi mulaakaat kaa avasar milegaa
 The comments singh ne kaha ki unhen dakshin korian raashtrapati lee myung-baak ke saath apni dwipaksheeya mulaakaat kaa bhi intjaar he

 donon kii mulaakaat ke baad ek sanyukt vaktavy jari kiya jayega

" hamaare bich vyapaar va nivesh kaa jeevant sambandh he

 babu jagjivan ram 6 krishna menon maarg ke is ghar main 1986 main apni mrityu tak rahaa karte the
